 299 |     |     /*:.+.*.*:.*..:..*.*:.*..:.+.*.*:*/
 300 |     |     /*           CLONES WITH IMMUTABLE ARGS OPERATIONS            */
 301 |     |     /*.:.+.*.:*.*.+.:*.*..:.:.*.:*.+.*/
 302 |     | 
 303 |     |     /// @dev Deploys a minimal proxy with `implementation`,
 304 |     |     /// using immutable arguments encoded in `data`.
 305 |     |     ///
 306 |     |     /// Note: This implementation of CWIA differs from the original implementation.
 307 |     |     /// If the calldata is empty, it will emit a `ReceiveETH(uint256)` event and skip the `DELEGATECALL`.
 308 |     |     function clone(address implementation, bytes memory data) internal returns (address instance) {
 309 |     |         assembly {
 310 |     |             // Compute the boundaries of the data and cache the memory slots around it.
 311 |     |             let mBefore3 := mload(sub(data, 0x60))
 312 |     |             let mBefore2 := mload(sub(data, 0x40))
 313 |     |             let mBefore1 := mload(sub(data, 0x20))
 314 |     |             let dataLength := mload(data)
 315 |     |             let dataEnd := add(add(data, 0x20), dataLength)
 316 |     |             let mAfter1 := mload(dataEnd)
 317 |     | 
 318 |     |             // +2 bytes for telling how much data there is appended to the call.
 319 |     |             let extraLength := add(dataLength, 2)
 320 |     |             // The `creationSize` is `extraLength + 108`
 321 |     |             // The `runSize` is `creationSize - 10`.
 322 |     | 
 323 |     |             /**
 324 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
 325 |     |              * CREATION (10 bytes)                                                                                |
 326 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
 327 |     |              * Opcode     | Mnemonic          | Stack     | Memory                                                |
 328 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
 329 |     |              * 61 runSize | PUSH2 runSize     | r         |                                                       |
 330 |     |              * 3d         | RETURNDATASIZE    | 0 r       |                                                       |
 331 |     |              * 81         | DUP2              | r 0 r     |                                                       |
 332 |     |              * 60 offset  | PUSH1 offset      | o r 0 r   |                                                       |
 333 |     |              * 3d         | RETURNDATASIZE    | 0 o r 0 r |                                                       |
 334 |     |              * 39         | CODECOPY          | 0 r       | [0..runSize): runtime code                            |
 335 |     |              * f3         | RETURN            |           | [0..runSize): runtime code                            |
 336 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
 337 |     |              * RUNTIME (98 bytes + extraLength)                                                                   |
 338 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
 339 |     |              * Opcode   | Mnemonic       | Stack                    | Memory                                      |
 340 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
 341 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 342 |     |              * ::: if no calldata, emit event & return w/o `DELEGATECALL` ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 343 |     |              * 36       | CALLDATASIZE   | cds                      |                                             |
 344 |     |              * 60 0x2c  | PUSH1 0x2c     | 0x2c cds                 |                                             |
 345 |     |              * 57       | JUMPI          |                          |                                             |
 346 |     |              * 34       | CALLVALUE      | cv                       |                                             |
 347 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 cv                     |                                             |
 348 |     |              * 52       | MSTORE         |                          | [0..0x20): callvalue                        |
 349 |     |              * 7f sig   | PUSH32 0x9e..  | sig                      | [0..0x20): callvalue                        |
 350 |     |              * 59       | MSIZE          | 0x20 sig                 | [0..0x20): callvalue                        |
 351 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 0x20 sig               | [0..0x20): callvalue                        |
 352 |     |              * a1       | LOG1           |                          | [0..0x20): callvalue                        |
 353 |     |              * 00       | STOP           |                          | [0..0x20): callvalue                        |
 354 |     |              * 5b       | JUMPDEST       |                          |                                             |
 355 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 356 |     |              * ::: copy calldata to memory :::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 357 |     |              * 36       | CALLDATASIZE   | cds                      |                                             |
 358 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 cds                    |                                             |
 359 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 0 cds                  |                                             |
 360 |     |              * 37       | CALLDATACOPY   |                          | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 361 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 362 |     |              * ::: keep some values in stack :::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 363 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0                        | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 364 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 0                      | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 365 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 0 0                    | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 366 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 0 0 0                  | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 367 |     |              * 61 extra | PUSH2 extra    | e 0 0 0 0                | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 368 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 369 |     |              * ::: copy extra data to memory :::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 370 |     |              * 80       | DUP1           | e e 0 0 0 0              | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 371 |     |              * 60 0x62  | PUSH1 0x62     | 0x62 e e 0 0 0 0         | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 372 |     |              * 36       | CALLDATASIZE   | cds 0x62 e e 0 0 0 0     | [0..cds): calldata                          |
 373 |     |              * 39       | CODECOPY       | e 0 0 0 0                | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 374 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 375 |     |              * ::: delegate call to the implementation contract ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 376 |     |              * 36       | CALLDATASIZE   | cds e 0 0 0 0            | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 377 |     |              * 01       | ADD            | cds+e 0 0 0 0            | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 378 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | 0 cds+e 0 0 0 0          | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 379 |     |              * 73 addr  | PUSH20 addr    | addr 0 cds+e 0 0 0 0     | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 380 |     |              * 5a       | GAS            | gas addr 0 cds+e 0 0 0 0 | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 381 |     |              * f4       | DELEGATECALL   | success 0 0              | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 382 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 383 |     |              * ::: copy return data to memory ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 384 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | rds success 0 0          | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 385 |     |              * 3d       | RETURNDATASIZE | rds rds success 0 0      | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 386 |     |              * 93       | SWAP4          | 0 rds success 0 rds      | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 387 |     |              * 80       | DUP1           | 0 0 rds success 0 rds    | [0..cds): calldata, [cds..cds+e): extraData |
 388 |     |              * 3e       | RETURNDATACOPY | success 0 rds            | [0..rds): returndata                        |
 389 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 390 |     |              * 60 0x60  | PUSH1 0x60     | 0x60 success 0 rds       | [0..rds): returndata                        |
 391 |     |              * 57       | JUMPI          | 0 rds                    | [0..rds): returndata                        |
 392 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 393 |     |              * ::: revert ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 394 |     |              * fd       | REVERT         |                          | [0..rds): returndata                        |
 395 |     |              *                                                                                                    |
 396 |     |              * ::: return ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: |
 397 |     |              * 5b       | JUMPDEST       | 0 rds                    | [0..rds): returndata                        |
 398 |     |              * f3       | RETURN         |                          | [0..rds): returndata                        |
 399 |     |              * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
 400 |     |              */
 401 |     |             // Write the bytecode before the data.
 402 |     |             mstore(data, 0x5af43d3d93803e606057fd5bf3)
 403 |     |             // Write the address of the implementation.
 404 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x0d), implementation)
 405 |     |             // Write the rest of the bytecode.
 406 |     |             mstore(
 407 |     |                 sub(data, 0x21),
 408 |     |                 or(shl(0x48, extraLength), 0x593da1005b363d3d373d3d3d3d610000806062363936013d73)
 409 |     |             )
 410 |     |             // `keccak256("ReceiveETH(uint256)")`
 411 |     |             mstore(
 412 |     |                 sub(data, 0x3a), 0x9e4ac34f21c619cefc926c8bd93b54bf5a39c7ab2127a895af1cc0691d7e3dff
 413 |     |             )
 414 |     |             mstore(
 415 |     |                 // Do a out-of-gas revert if `extraLength` is too big. 0xffff - 0x62 + 0x01 = 0xff9e.
 416 |     |                 // The actual EVM limit may be smaller and may change over time.
 417 |     |                 sub(data, add(0x59, lt(extraLength, 0xff9e))),
 418 |     |                 or(shl(0x78, add(extraLength, 0x62)), 0xfd6100003d81600a3d39f336602c57343d527f)
 419 |     |             )
 420 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, shl(0xf0, extraLength))
 421 |     | 
 422 |     |             // Create the instance.
 423 |     |             instance := create(0, sub(data, 0x4c), add(extraLength, 0x6c))
 424 |     | 
 425 |     |             // If `instance` is zero, revert.
 426 |     |             if iszero(instance) {
 427 |     |                 // Store the function selector of `DeploymentFailed()`.
 428 |     |                 mstore(0x00, 0x30116425)
 429 |     |                 // Revert with (offset, size).
 430 |     |                 revert(0x1c, 0x04)
 431 |     |             }
 432 |     | 
 433 |     |             // Restore the overwritten memory surrounding `data`.
 434 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, mAfter1)
 435 |     |             mstore(data, dataLength)
 436 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x20), mBefore1)
 437 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x40), mBefore2)
 438 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x60), mBefore3)
 439 |     |         }
 440 |     |     }
 441 |     | 
 442 |     |     /// @dev Deploys a deterministic clone of `implementation`,
 443 |     |     /// using immutable arguments encoded in `data`, with `salt`.
 444 |     |     ///
 445 |     |     /// Note: This implementation of CWIA differs from the original implementation.
 446 |     |     /// If the calldata is empty, it will emit a `ReceiveETH(uint256)` event and skip the `DELEGATECALL`.
 447 |     |     function cloneDeterministic(address implementation, bytes memory data, bytes32 salt)
 448 |     |         internal
 449 |     |         returns (address instance)
 450 |     |     {
 451 |     |         assembly {
 452 |     |             // Compute the boundaries of the data and cache the memory slots around it.
 453 |     |             let mBefore3 := mload(sub(data, 0x60))
 454 |     |             let mBefore2 := mload(sub(data, 0x40))
 455 |     |             let mBefore1 := mload(sub(data, 0x20))
 456 |     |             let dataLength := mload(data)
 457 |     |             let dataEnd := add(add(data, 0x20), dataLength)
 458 |     |             let mAfter1 := mload(dataEnd)
 459 |     | 
 460 |     |             // +2 bytes for telling how much data there is appended to the call.
 461 |     |             let extraLength := add(dataLength, 2)
 462 |     | 
 463 |     |             // Write the bytecode before the data.
 464 |     |             mstore(data, 0x5af43d3d93803e606057fd5bf3)
 465 |     |             // Write the address of the implementation.
 466 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x0d), implementation)
 467 |     |             // Write the rest of the bytecode.
 468 |     |             mstore(
 469 |     |                 sub(data, 0x21),
 470 |     |                 or(shl(0x48, extraLength), 0x593da1005b363d3d373d3d3d3d610000806062363936013d73)
 471 |     |             )
 472 |     |             // `keccak256("ReceiveETH(uint256)")`
 473 |     |             mstore(
 474 |     |                 sub(data, 0x3a), 0x9e4ac34f21c619cefc926c8bd93b54bf5a39c7ab2127a895af1cc0691d7e3dff
 475 |     |             )
 476 |     |             mstore(
 477 |     |                 // Do a out-of-gas revert if `extraLength` is too big. 0xffff - 0x62 + 0x01 = 0xff9e.
 478 |     |                 // The actual EVM limit may be smaller and may change over time.
 479 |     |                 sub(data, add(0x59, lt(extraLength, 0xff9e))),
 480 |     |                 or(shl(0x78, add(extraLength, 0x62)), 0xfd6100003d81600a3d39f336602c57343d527f)
 481 |     |             )
 482 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, shl(0xf0, extraLength))
 483 |     | 
 484 |     |             // Create the instance.
 485 |     |             instance := create2(0, sub(data, 0x4c), add(extraLength, 0x6c), salt)
 486 |     | 
 487 |     |             // If `instance` is zero, revert.
 488 |     |             if iszero(instance) {
 489 |     |                 // Store the function selector of `DeploymentFailed()`.
 490 |     |                 mstore(0x00, 0x30116425)
 491 |     |                 // Revert with (offset, size).
 492 |     |                 revert(0x1c, 0x04)
 493 |     |             }
 494 |     | 
 495 |     |             // Restore the overwritten memory surrounding `data`.
 496 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, mAfter1)
 497 |     |             mstore(data, dataLength)
 498 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x20), mBefore1)
 499 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x40), mBefore2)
 500 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x60), mBefore3)
 501 |     |         }
 502 |     |     }
 503 |     | 
 504 |     |     /// @dev Returns the initialization code hash of the clone of `implementation`
 505 |     |     /// using immutable arguments encoded in `data`.
 506 |     |     /// Used for mining vanity addresses with create2crunch.
 507 |     |     function initCodeHash(address implementation, bytes memory data)
 508 |     |         internal
 509 |     |         pure
 510 |     |         returns (bytes32 hash)
 511 |     |     {
 512 |     |         assembly {
 513 |     |             // Compute the boundaries of the data and cache the memory slots around it.
 514 |     |             let mBefore3 := mload(sub(data, 0x60))
 515 |     |             let mBefore2 := mload(sub(data, 0x40))
 516 |     |             let mBefore1 := mload(sub(data, 0x20))
 517 |     |             let dataLength := mload(data)
 518 |     |             let dataEnd := add(add(data, 0x20), dataLength)
 519 |     |             let mAfter1 := mload(dataEnd)
 520 |     | 
 521 |     |             // Do a out-of-gas revert if `dataLength` is too big. 0xffff - 0x02 - 0x62 = 0xff9b.
 522 |     |             // The actual EVM limit may be smaller and may change over time.
 523 |     |             returndatacopy(returndatasize(), returndatasize(), gt(dataLength, 0xff9b))
 524 |     | 
 525 |     |             // +2 bytes for telling how much data there is appended to the call.
 526 |     |             let extraLength := add(dataLength, 2)
 527 |     | 
 528 |     |             // Write the bytecode before the data.
 529 |     |             mstore(data, 0x5af43d3d93803e606057fd5bf3)
 530 |     |             // Write the address of the implementation.
 531 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x0d), implementation)
 532 |     |             // Write the rest of the bytecode.
 533 |     |             mstore(
 534 |     |                 sub(data, 0x21),
 535 |     |                 or(shl(0x48, extraLength), 0x593da1005b363d3d373d3d3d3d610000806062363936013d73)
 536 |     |             )
 537 |     |             // `keccak256("ReceiveETH(uint256)")`
 538 |     |             mstore(
 539 |     |                 sub(data, 0x3a), 0x9e4ac34f21c619cefc926c8bd93b54bf5a39c7ab2127a895af1cc0691d7e3dff
 540 |     |             )
 541 |     |             mstore(
 542 |     |                 sub(data, 0x5a),
 543 |     |                 or(shl(0x78, add(extraLength, 0x62)), 0x6100003d81600a3d39f336602c57343d527f)
 544 |     |             )
 545 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, shl(0xf0, extraLength))
 546 |     | 
 547 |     |             // Compute and store the bytecode hash.
 548 |     |             hash := keccak256(sub(data, 0x4c), add(extraLength, 0x6c))
 549 |     | 
 550 |     |             // Restore the overwritten memory surrounding `data`.
 551 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, mAfter1)
 552 |     |             mstore(data, dataLength)
 553 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x20), mBefore1)
 554 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x40), mBefore2)
 555 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x60), mBefore3)
 556 |     |         }
 557 |     |     }
 558 |     | 
 559 |     |     /// @dev Returns the address of the deterministic clone of
 560 |     |     /// `implementation` using immutable arguments encoded in `data`, with `salt`, by `deployer`.
 561 |     |     /// Note: The returned result has dirty upper 96 bits. Please clean if used in assembly.
 562 |     |     function predictDeterministicAddress(
 563 |     |         address implementation,
 564 |     |         bytes memory data,
 565 |     |         bytes32 salt,
 566 |     |         address deployer
 567 |     |     ) internal pure returns (address predicted) {
 568 |     |         bytes32 hash = initCodeHash(implementation, data);
 569 |     |         predicted = predictDeterministicAddress(hash, salt, deployer);
 570 |     |     }
 571 |     | 
 572 |     |     /*:.+.*.*:.*..:..*.*:.*..:.+.*.*:*/
 573 |     |     /*                      OTHER OPERATIONS                      */
 574 |     |     /*.:.+.*.:*.*.+.:*.*..:.:.*.:*.+.*/
 575 |     | 
 576 |     |     /// @dev Returns the address when a contract with initialization code hash,
 577 |     |     /// `hash`, is deployed with `salt`, by `deployer`.
 578 |     |     /// Note: The returned result has dirty upper 96 bits. Please clean if used in assembly.
 579 |     |     function predictDeterministicAddress(bytes32 hash, bytes32 salt, address deployer)
 580 |     |         internal
 581 |     |         pure
 582 |     |         returns (address predicted)
 583 |     |     {
 584 |     |         /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
 585 |     |         assembly {
 586 |     |             // Compute and store the bytecode hash.
 587 |     |             mstore8(0x00, 0xff) // Write the prefix.
 588 |     |             mstore(0x35, hash)
 589 |     |             mstore(0x01, shl(96, deployer))
 590 |     |             mstore(0x15, salt)
 591 |     |             predicted := keccak256(0x00, 0x55)
 592 |     |             // Restore the part of the free memory pointer that has been overwritten.
 593 |     |             mstore(0x35, 0)
 594 |     |         }
 595 |     |     }
 596 |     | 
 597 |     |     /// @dev Reverts if `salt` does not start with either the zero address or the caller.
 598 |     |     function checkStartsWithCaller(bytes32 salt) internal view {
 599 |     |         /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
 600 |     |         assembly {
 601 |     |             // If the salt does not start with the zero address or the caller.
 602 |     |             if iszero(or(iszero(shr(96, salt)), eq(caller(), shr(96, salt)))) {
 603 |     |                 // Store the function selector of `SaltDoesNotStartWithCaller()`.
 604 |     |                 mstore(0x00, 0x2f634836)
 605 |     |                 // Revert with (offset, size).
 606 |     |                 revert(0x1c, 0x04)
 607 |     |             }
 608 |     |         }
 609 |     |     }
 610 |     | }

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0

   4 |     | import {Clone} from '@solady/utils/Clone.sol';

  13 | *r  | contract VestingEscrow is IVestingEscrow, Clone {

  15 |     |     using Address for address;
  16 |     |     using Address for address payable;
  17 |     | 
  18 |     |     /// @notice The factory that created this VestingEscrow instance.
  19 | *   |     function factory() public pure returns (IVestingEscrowFactory) {
  20 | *   |         return IVestingEscrowFactory(_getArgAddress(0));
  21 |     |     }
  22 |     | 
  23 |     |     /// @notice The token.
  24 | *   |     function token() public pure returns (IERC20) {

  26 |     |     }
  27 |     | 
  28 |     |     /// @notice The token recipient.
  29 | *   |     function recipient() public pure returns (address) {
  30 | *   |         return _getArgAddress(40);
  31 |     |     }
  32 |     | 
  33 |     |     /// @notice The vesting start timestamp.
  34 | *   |     function startTime() public pure returns (uint40) {
  35 | *   |         return _getArgUint40(60);
  36 |     |     }
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |     /// @notice The vesting end timestamp.
  39 | *   |     function endTime() public pure returns (uint40) {
  40 | *   |         return _getArgUint40(65);
  41 |     |     }
  42 |     | 
  43 |     |     /// @notice The vesting cliff length.
  44 | *   |     function cliffLength() public pure returns (uint40) {
  45 | *   |         return _getArgUint40(70);

 274 |     |     /// @dev Returns the vested token amount at a specific time.

 277 | *   |         uint40 _startTime = startTime();

 280 | *   |             return 0;

 282 | *   |         return Math.min(_totalLocked * (time - _startTime) / (endTime() - _startTime), _totalLocked);

/mnt/f/Projects/audits/rio-vesting-escrow/src/VestingEscrowFactory.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.23;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import {LibClone} from '@solady/utils/LibClone.sol';
   5 |     | import {Address} from '@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Address.sol';
   6 |     | import {Ownable} from '@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol';
   7 |     | import {IERC20} from '@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol';
   8 |     | import {Ownable2Step} from '@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable2Step.sol';
   9 |     | import {SafeERC20} from '@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/utils/SafeERC20.sol';
  10 |     | import {IVestingEscrowFactory} from 'src/interfaces/IVestingEscrowFactory.sol';
  11 |     | import {IVestingEscrow} from 'src/interfaces/IVestingEscrow.sol';
  12 |     | 
  13 |     | contract VestingEscrowFactory is IVestingEscrowFactory, Ownable2Step {
  14 |     |     using LibClone for address;
  15 |     |     using SafeERC20 for IERC20;
  16 |     |     using Address for address payable;
  17 |     | 
  18 |     |     /// @notice The vesting escrow implementation contract.
  19 |     |     address public immutable vestingEscrowImpl;
  20 |     | 
  21 |     |     /// @notice The ERC20 token that will be locked in the vesting contracts.
  22 |     |     address public immutable token;
  23 |     | 
  24 |     |     /// @notice The adaptor that will be used to delegate and/or vote from the vesting contracts.
  25 |     |     address public votingAdaptor;
  26 |     | 
  27 |     |     /// @notice The account that will manage the vesting contracts.
  28 |     |     address public manager;
  29 |     | 
  30 |     |     constructor(address _vestingEscrowImpl, address _token, address _owner, address _manager, address _votingAdaptor) {
  31 |     |         if (_vestingEscrowImpl == address(0)) revert INVALID_VESTING_ESCROW_IMPL();
  32 |     |         if (_token == address(0)) revert INVALID_TOKEN();
  33 |     |         if (_owner == address(0)) revert INVALID_OWNER();
  34 |     | 
  35 |     |         vestingEscrowImpl = _vestingEscrowImpl;
  36 |     |         token = _token;
  37 |     |         manager = _manager;
  38 |     |         votingAdaptor = _votingAdaptor;
  39 |     | 
  40 |     |         _transferOwnership(_owner);
  41 |     |     }
  42 |     | 
  43 |     |     /// @notice Deploy and fund a new vesting contract.
  44 |     |     /// @param amount The amount of tokens to lock in the vesting contract.
  45 |     |     /// @param recipient The recipient of the vesting contract.
  46 |     |     /// @param vestingDuration The duration of the vesting contract.
  47 |     |     /// @param vestingStart The start of the vesting contract.
  48 |     |     /// @param cliffLength The cliff length of the vesting contract.
  49 |     |     /// @param isFullyRevokable Whether the vesting contract is fully revokable.
  50 |     |     /// @param initialDelegateParams The optional initial delegate information (skipped if empty bytes).
  51 |     |     function deployVestingContract(
  52 |     |         uint256 amount,
  53 |     |         address recipient,
  54 |     |         uint40 vestingDuration,
  55 |     |         uint40 vestingStart,
  56 |     |         uint40 cliffLength,
  57 |     |         bool isFullyRevokable,
  58 |     |         bytes calldata initialDelegateParams
  59 |     |     ) external returns (address escrow) {
  60 |     |         if (vestingDuration == 0) revert INVALID_VESTING_DURATION();
  61 |     |         if (cliffLength > vestingDuration) revert INVALID_VESTING_CLIFF();
  62 |     |         if (recipient == address(0)) revert INVALID_RECIPIENT();
  63 |     |         if (amount == 0) revert INVALID_AMOUNT();
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |         escrow = vestingEscrowImpl.clone(
  66 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
  67 |     |                 address(this), token, recipient, vestingStart, vestingStart + vestingDuration, cliffLength, amount
  68 |     |             )
  69 |     |         );
  70 |     | 
  71 |     |         IERC20(token).safeTransferFrom(msg.sender, escrow, amount);
  72 |     |         IVestingEscrow(escrow).initialize(isFullyRevokable, initialDelegateParams);
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |         emit VestingEscrowCreated(msg.sender, recipient, escrow);
  75 |     |     }
  76 |     | 
  77 |     |     /// @notice Recover any ERC20 to the owner.
  78 |     |     /// @param token_ The ERC20 token to recover.
  79 |     |     /// @param amount The amount to recover.
  80 |     |     function recoverERC20(address token_, uint256 amount) external {
  81 |     |         if (amount > 0) {
  82 |     |             IERC20(token_).safeTransfer(owner(), amount);
  83 |     |             emit ERC20Recovered(token_, amount);
  84 |     |         }
  85 |     |     }
  86 |     | 
  87 |     |     /// @notice Recover any ETH to the owner.
  88 |     |     function recoverEther() external {
  89 |     |         uint256 amount = address(this).balance;
  90 |     |         if (amount > 0) {
  91 |     |             payable(owner()).sendValue(amount);
  92 |     |             emit ETHRecovered(amount);
  93 |     |         }
  94 |     |     }
  95 |     | 
  96 |     |     /// @notice Change the voting adaptor of the vesting contracts.
  97 |     |     function updateVotingAdaptor(address _votingAdaptor) external onlyOwner {
  98 |     |         votingAdaptor = _votingAdaptor;
  99 |     |         emit VotingAdaptorUpgraded(_votingAdaptor);
 100 |     |     }
 101 |     | 
 102 |     |     /// @notice Change the manager of the vesting contracts.
 103 |     |     function changeManager(address _manager) external onlyOwner {
 104 |     |         manager = _manager;
 105 |     |         emit ManagerChanged(_manager);
 106 |     |     }
 107 |     | 
 108 |     |     /// @notice The address of the current owner.
 109 |     |     function owner() public view override(Ownable, IVestingEscrowFactory) returns (address) {
 110 |     |         return super.owner();
 111 |     |     }
 112 |     | 
 113 |     |         event AssertionFailed(uint256);
 114 |     |     event AssertionFailed();
 115 |     |     event AssertionFailed(string);
 116 |     | }

/mnt/f/Projects/audits/rio-vesting-escrow/src/interfaces/IVestingEscrow.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0
  2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.23;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | interface IVestingEscrow {
  5 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the caller is not the owner.
  6 |     |     error NOT_OWNER(address account);
  7 |     | 
  8 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the caller is not the owner or manager.
  9 |     |     error NOT_OWNER_OR_MANAGER(address account);
 10 |     | 
 11 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the caller is not the recipient.
 12 |     |     error NOT_RECIPIENT(address account);
 13 |     | 
 14 |     |     /// @notice Throws if called by any account other than the factory.
 15 |     |     error NOT_FACTORY(address account);
 16 |     | 
 17 |     |     /// @notice Throws if the contract token balance is insufficient.
 18 |     |     error INSUFFICIENT_BALANCE();
 19 |     | 
 20 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when tokens are not fully revokable.
 21 |     |     error NOT_FULLY_REVOKABLE();
 22 |     | 
 23 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when tokens are already fully revoked.
 24 |     |     error ALREADY_FULLY_REVOKED();
 25 |     | 
 26 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when there are no tokens to revoke.
 27 |     |     error NOTHING_TO_REVOKE();
 28 |     | 
 29 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the voting adaptor is not set.
 30 |     |     error VOTING_ADAPTOR_NOT_SET();
 31 |     | 
 32 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when the vesting escrow is initialized.
 33 |     |     event VestingEscrowInitialized(
 34 |     |         address indexed factory,
 35 |     |         address indexed recipient,
 36 |     |         address indexed token,
 37 |     |         uint256 amount,
 38 |     |         uint40 startTime,
 39 |     |         uint40 endTime,
 40 |     |         uint40 cliffLength,
 41 |     |         bool isFullyRevokable
 42 |     |     );
 43 |     | 
 44 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when vested tokens are claimed.
 45 |     |     event Claim(address indexed beneficiary, uint256 claimed);
 46 |     | 
 47 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when unvested tokens are revoked.
 48 |     |     event UnvestedTokensRevoked(address indexed recoverer, uint256 revoked);
 49 |     | 
 50 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when all tokens are revoked.
 51 |     |     event VestingFullyRevoked(address indexed recoverer, uint256 revoked);
 52 |     | 
 53 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when full revocation power is permanently disabled.
 54 |     |     event FullRevocationPermanentlyDisabled(address indexed owner);
 55 |     | 
 56 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when ERC20 tokens are recovered.
 57 |     |     event ERC20Recovered(address token, uint256 amount);
 58 |     | 
 59 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when ETH is recovered.
 60 |     |     event ETHRecovered(uint256 amount);
 61 |     | 
 62 |     |     /// @notice Initializes the contract.
 63 |     |     /// @param isFullyRevokable Whether the tokens are fully revokable.
 64 |     |     /// @param initialDelegateParams The optional initial delegate information (skipped if empty bytes).
 65 |     |     function initialize(bool isFullyRevokable, bytes calldata initialDelegateParams) external;
 66 |     | }
 67 |     | 

/mnt/f/Projects/audits/rio-vesting-escrow/src/interfaces/IVestingEscrowFactory.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0
  2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.23;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | interface IVestingEscrowFactory {
  5 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the vesting duration is zero
  6 |     |     error INVALID_VESTING_DURATION();
  7 |     | 
  8 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the vesting cliff is greater than the vesting duration
  9 |     |     error INVALID_VESTING_CLIFF();
 10 |     | 
 11 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the recipient is the zero address
 12 |     |     error INVALID_RECIPIENT();
 13 |     | 
 14 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the amount is zero
 15 |     |     error INVALID_AMOUNT();
 16 |     | 
 17 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the vesting escrow implementation is the zero address
 18 |     |     error INVALID_VESTING_ESCROW_IMPL();
 19 |     | 
 20 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the token is the zero address
 21 |     |     error INVALID_TOKEN();
 22 |     | 
 23 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the owner is the zero address
 24 |     |     error INVALID_OWNER();
 25 |     | 
 26 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when a transfer fails.
 27 |     |     error TRANSFER_FAILED();
 28 |     | 
 29 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when a vesting escrow is created.
 30 |     |     event VestingEscrowCreated(address indexed creator, address indexed recipient, address escrow);
 31 |     | 
 32 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when an ERC20 token is recovered.
 33 |     |     event ERC20Recovered(address token, uint256 amount);
 34 |     | 
 35 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when ETH is recovered.
 36 |     |     event ETHRecovered(uint256 amount);
 37 |     | 
 38 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when the voting adaptor is upgraded.
 39 |     |     event VotingAdaptorUpgraded(address votingAdaptor);
 40 |     | 
 41 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when the manager is changed.
 42 |     |     event ManagerChanged(address manager);
 43 |     | 
 44 |     |     function votingAdaptor() external view returns (address);
 45 |     |     function owner() external view returns (address);
 46 |     |     function manager() external view returns (address);
 47 |     | }

/mnt/f/Projects/audits/rio-vesting-escrow/src/interfaces/IVotingAdaptor.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0
  2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.23;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | interface IVotingAdaptor {
  5 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the owner is the zero address.
  6 |     |     error INVALID_OWNER();
  7 |     | 
  8 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the governor is the zero address.
  9 |     |     error INVALID_GOVERNOR();
 10 |     | 
 11 |     |     /// @notice Thrown when the voting token is the zero address.
 12 |     |     error INVALID_VOTING_TOKEN();
 13 |     | 
 14 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when ERC20 tokens are recovered.
 15 |     |     event ERC20Recovered(address token, uint256 amount);
 16 |     | 
 17 |     |     /// @notice Emitted when ETH is recovered.
 18 |     |     event ETHRecovered(uint256 amount);
 19 |     | 
 20 |     |     /// @notice Delegate votes.
 21 |     |     /// @param params The ABI-encoded delegate params.
 22 |     |     function delegate(bytes calldata params) external;
 23 |     | 
 24 |     |     /// @notice Vote on a proposal.
 25 |     |     /// @param params The ABI-encoded vote params.
 26 |     |     function vote(bytes calldata params) external;
 27 |     | 
 28 |     |     /// @notice Vote on a proposal with a reason.
 29 |     |     /// @param params The ABI-encoded vote with reason params.
 30 |     |     function voteWithReason(bytes calldata params) external;

  1 |     | // // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0
  2 |     | // pragma solidity 0.8.23;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | // import {TestUtil} from 'test/lib/TestUtil.sol';
  5 |     | // import {ERC20Token} from 'test/lib/ERC20Token.sol';
  6 |     | 
  7 |     | // contract VestingEscrowFactoryTest is TestUtil {
  8 |     | //     function setUp() public {
  9 |     | //         setUpProtocol(ProtocolConfig({owner: address(1), manager: address(2)}));
 10 |     | //         deployVestingEscrow(
 11 |     | //             VestingEscrowConfig({
 12 |     | //                 amount: 1 ether,
 13 |     | //                 recipient: address(this),
 14 |     | //                 vestingDuration: 365 days,
 15 |     | //                 vestingStart: uint40(block.timestamp),
 16 |     | //                 cliffLength: 90 days,
 17 |     | //                 isFullyRevokable: true,
 18 |     | //                 initialDelegateParams: new bytes(0)
 19 |     | //             })
 20 |     | //         );
 21 |     | //     }
 22 |     | 
 23 |     | //     function testRecoverERC20() public {
 24 |     | //         ERC20Token token2 = new ERC20Token();
 25 |     | //         address _owner = factory.owner();
 26 |     | 
 27 |     | //         token2.mint(address(factory), amount);
 28 |     |
